The filter may need to handle\n60:   // watermark events when injecting a body, see:\n61:   // https://github.com/envoyproxy/envoy/blob/main/source/docs/flow_control.md.\n62:   //\n63:   // The last call to inject data MUST have end_stream set to true to conclude the stream.\n64:   // If the filter cannot provide a body the stream should be reset.\n65:   //\n66:   // Adding a body through calling addDecodedData()/addEncodedData() then\n67:   // continueDecoding()/continueEncoding() is currently NOT supported and causes an assert failure.\n68:   //\n69:   // Adding trailers in this scenario is currently NOT supported.\n70:   //\n71:   // The filter MUST NOT attempt to continue the stream without providing a body using\n72:   // continueDecoding()/continueEncoding().\n73:   //\n74:   // TODO(yosrym93): Support adding a body in this case by calling addDecodedData()/addEncodedData()\n75:   // then continueDecoding()/continueEncoding(). This causes ASSERTs in\n79:   // FilterManager::commonContinue() to fail when continueDecoding()/continueEncoding() is called;\n80:   // due to trying to continue iteration when the IterationState is already Continue.\n81:   // In this case, a different ASSERT will be needed to make sure the filter does not try to\n82:   // continue without adding a body first.\n83:   //\n84:   // TODO(yosrym93): Support adding trailers in this case by implementing new functions to inject\n85:   // trailers, similar to the inject data functions.\n86:   ContinueAndDontEndStream,\n87:   // Do not iterate for headers as well as data and trailers for the current filter and the filters\n88:   // following, and buffer body data for later dispatching. ContinueDecoding() MUST\n89:   // be called if continued filter iteration is desired.\n90:   //\n91:   // Used when a filter wants to stop iteration on data and trailers while waiting for headers'\n92:   // iteration to resume.\n93:   //\n94:   // If buffering the request causes buffered data to exceed the configured buffer limit, a 413 will\n95:   // be sent to the user. On the response path exceeding buffer limits will result in a 500.\n96:   //\n97:   // TODO(soya3129): stop metadata parsing when StopAllIterationAndBuffer is set.\n98:   StopAllIterationAndBuffer,\n99:   // Do not iterate for headers as well as data and trailers for the current filter and the filters\n100:   // following, and buffer body data for later dispatching. continueDecoding() MUST\n101: ","url":"https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/github.com/sg-evals/envoy--v1.31.2@9fad78c5ca13df58ab7b58c0918b8986c9f01efb/-/blob/envoy/http/filter.h%3FL1-100"}}}

chain extension mechanism in Envoy is composed of three major components:\\n\\n1. **Filter Factory Registry**: Handles registration and discovery of HTTP filters\\n2. **Filter Context**: Provides metadata about filter configuration during chain creation\\n3. **Per-Request Filter Chain Execution**: Manages runtime instantiation and execution of filters for each HTTP stream\\n\\n## Core Files\\n\\n### Filter Factory Interfaces (envoy/http/filter_factory.h)\\nDefines the core abstractions for HTTP filter chain management:\\n- `FilterFactoryCb`: Type alias for a function that accepts `FilterChainFactoryCallbacks` and creates filter instances\\n- `FilterContext`: Struct containing filter configuration name and extension qualified name\\n- `FilterChainManager`: Interface allowing filter factories to apply filter factory callbacks to a manager\\n- `FilterChainFactory`: Interface for creating HTTP filter chains when new streams are created\\n\\n### Filter Interfaces (envoy/http/filter.h)\\nDefines filter types and callbacks:\\n- `FilterChainFactoryCallbacks`: Interface that filter factories use to add filters to the chain\\n- `StreamFilter`: Base interface for HTTP filters\\n- `StreamDecoderFilter`: Interface for decoding path filters\\n- `StreamEncoderFilter`: Interface for encoding path filters\\n\\n### Filter Configuration Registry (envoy/server/filter_config.h)\\nDefines factory interfaces for filter registration:\\n- `HttpFilterConfigFactoryBase`: Base factory class with protocol options support\\n- `NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory`: Factory interface for downstream HTTP filters; registered in the registry\\n- `UpstreamHttpFilterConfigFactory`: Factory interface for upstream HTTP filters to clusters\\n- These factories implement `createFilterFactoryFromProto()` to convert protobuf config into `FilterFactoryCb` functions\\n\\n## Implementation Files\\n\\n### Filter Manager (source/common/http/filter_manager.h and .cc)\\nThe per-request filter chain execution engine:\\n- `FilterManager`: Main implementation managing active filters in a stream\\n- `FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl`: Nested class implementing `FilterChainFactoryCallbacks` interface\\n- Manages decoder/encoder filter lists and iteration state\\n- Implements `applyFilterFactoryCb()` to execute filter factory callbacks\\n- Invokes filters in the correct order (decoder path, then encoder path)\\n\\n### Filter Chain Helper (source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h and .cc)\\nStateful filter chain factory support:\\n- `FilterChainUtility`: Static utility for creating HTTP filter chains from factory lists\\n  - `createFilterChainForFactories()`: Converts filter factory callbacks into active filter instances\\n  - `FilterFactoryProvider`: Wraps a filter config provider and disabled status\\n  - `FilterFactoriesList`: List of filter factory providers\\n- `FilterChainHelper`: Template class for processing filter configurations\\n  - `processFilters()`: Converts protobuf filter configs into filter factory callbacks\\n  - Handles both static and dynamic (ECDS) filter configurations\\n  - Validates filter dependencies and terminal filter constraints\\n- Creates singleton `DownstreamFilterConfigProviderManager` and `UpstreamFilterConfigProviderManager`\\n\\n### Dynamic Filter Configuration (source/common/filter/config_discovery_impl.h and .cc)\\nSupport for dynamic filter discovery via ECDS:\\n- `HttpDynamicFilterConfigProviderImpl`: Template class implementing dynamic filter config provider\\n  - `instantiateFilterFactory()`: Converts protobuf messages to `NamedHttpFilterFactoryCb`\\n  - Supports both `NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory` and `UpstreamHttpFilterConfigFactory`\\n- Manages filter configuration subscription and warm-up\\n- Handles filter factory resolution from registry by type URL\\n\\n### Common Factory Base (source/extensions/filters/http/common/factory_base.h)\\nTemplate base class for filter factory implementations:\\n- `CommonFactoryBase`: Generic template implementing both `NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory` and `UpstreamHttpFilterConfigFactory`\\n- Provides `createFilterFactoryFromProtoTyped()` for type-safe factory creation\\n- Reduces boilerplate for individual filter implementations\\n\\n## Extension Points\\n\\nEach HTTP filter implements a factory class (e.g., `source/extensions/filters/http/*/config.h`) that:\\n1. Derives from `NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory` or `UpstreamHttpFilterConfigFactory` (or both)\\n2. Implements `createFilterFactoryFromProto()` to parse configuration and return a `FilterFactoryCb`\\n3. Registers itself via `REGISTER_FACTORY()` macro in the `NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory` registry\\n4. The returned `FilterFactoryCb` captures configuration state and creates filter instances on invocation\\n\\n## Execution Flow\\n\\n1. Configuration Phase:\\n   - Filter configurations are loaded via protobuf\\n   - `FilterChainHelper::processFilters()` looks up factories in registry\\n   - Each factory's `createFilterFactoryFromProto()` creates a `FilterFactoryCb` closure\\n   - Closures are stored in a `FilterFactoriesList`\\n\\n2. Stream Creation Phase:\\n   - `FilterChainFactory::createFilterChain()` is invoked per new HTTP stream\\n   - Calls `FilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories()` with the factory list\\n   - This function iterates through factories and calls `manager.applyFilterFactoryCb()`\\n\\n3. Filter Instantiation Phase:\\n   - `FilterManager::applyFilterFactoryCb()` invokes each `FilterFactoryCb` with a `FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl`\\n   - The closure executes its captured configuration and calls callbacks to add filters\\n   - Filters are added to appropriate lists (decoder filters, encoder filters)\\n\\n4. Stream Processing Phase:\\n   - `FilterManager` iterates through filters on headers, data, trailers\\n   - Respects filter return codes to control chain progression\\n   - Handles filter callbacks for headers/data injection and local replies\\n\\n## Key Design Patterns\\n\\n- **Factory Pattern**: Filter factories defer actual filter creation until stream time, enabling:\\n  - Configuration validation at startup\\n  - Lazy filter instantiation only for active streams\\n  - Filter instance per-stream isolation\\n\\n- **Callback-based Composition**: `FilterFactoryCb` closures capture configuration and create filters dynamically\\n\\n- **Registry Pattern**: `REGISTER_FACTORY()` enables dynamic filter discovery without compile-time dependencies\\n\\n- **Template Specialization**: `FilterChainHelper` and `HttpDynamicFilterConfigProviderImpl` use templates to handle both downstream and upstream contexts\\n\\n- **Visitor Pattern**: `FilterChainFactoryCallbacks` allows filters to be added without filter manager knowing specific filter types\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":3055,"cache_read_input_tokens":97073,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":3055},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"4f38395f-bfbb-4113-b891-621ec3fd29f2","uuid":"aa6ad64b-1708-47c3-a233-5b7c06b37f80"}
